3. Free fish food, which is the favorite of the children.
4. Free 2 kilograms of strawberry picking. Although the size of the strawberries is very average, the process of picking by the baby is worry-free.
5. When checking out, they will still ask about the experience of staying here, and those with children will continue to receive milk or juice.
6. If you are with your child, the service staff will take the initiative to give the parents lemonade [yeah], and you can also take care of it.
7. You can camp and barbecue.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Family Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:14 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 1, 2024
msg:The original hotel for the group building of the little kids was fully booked, so we temporarily changed to this one, 4 families and 4 kids, the group room + strawberry picking + naughty castle + cute pet park package. Because it was the first time to book this hotel, I was still a little nervous before going, but the overall experience was ideal.
Room: The family room in the American-style building. The hygiene is good, with a 1.5-meter bed and a single bed. The beds cannot be put together, so the mattress of the big bed can only be pushed to the wall. Although there are children's slippers, etc., the furniture lacks some child protection measures, and there is some decoration smell, and the window needs to be opened. In addition, in late March, the hotel air conditioning has stopped heating, and it is a bit cold at night. The waiter added an electric heater, but the effect is limited.
Hotel environment: The natural environment is very good, there is a large artificial lake, there are many koi, black swans, ducks, and the front desk delivers fish food, and the children are very happy to feed. There is a family of three ponies, rabbits, and groundhogs in the cute pet park. The carrots for feeding are 30 per serving, which is a bit expensive. Bamboo tubes are provided to help feed. The quality of non-powered facilities is also good. There are also a lot of lawns in the campus, which are very photogenic with buildings, windmills, flowers and plants of different appearances. I didn't experience the paid camping area, which is said to be open in April and May. The naughty castle on the second floor of the main building is small and large, with various slides, cassia seed sand pool, trampoline, ocean ball projection screen, and is open until 8 pm. The swimming pool on the first floor of the main building is open for a long time. Although the facilities are slightly old and the hot spring is not open, there is a children's pool with good water temperature, but the room temperature is cold. It is basically reserved on weekends. The baby learned to swim by himself in the hotel swimming pool, which is gratifying. Some areas of the hotel are still under renovation, and the construction quality is also very good. I hope to come again in summer.
Service: The parent-child service is still attentive. Children's snacks, milk, candy, fish food, etc. are given. The strawberry picking coupons are just opposite the hotel. The experience is satisfactory.
Catering: I experienced the hotel breakfast. The variety and quality are about 4 stars. The quality is acceptable, lacking characteristics, and there are many participants. The companions of the buffet dinner said it was average, and they could drive to other restaurants for dinner.
Overall evaluation: In terms of facilities, it is still a conference hotel. You can see a lot of conference participants in suits and ties on weekends. It also hosts wedding banquets, etc. However, since the hotel park is very large, it doesn't feel very crowded except at breakfast time. The parent-child facilities of the hotel are very cost-effective because there are few people. Coupled with the beautiful natural environment, the kids had a lot of fun. It is a treasure hotel.

msg:I accidentally searched online. The guest room buildings in various countries are very distinctive and cost-effective. The original petrochemical guesthouse has a slightly older decoration, but it is very good and fun overall, and the service is also good. There are many meeting rooms and banquet halls, suitable for meetings and wedding banquets. We booked a family room with a single bed and a double bed. The housekeeper service is very good. We called in advance and learned that we had elderly people with inconvenient legs and feet, so they were arranged on the first floor. We added WeChat to communicate at any time, and they would send reminders of activities and breakfast time, which was very considerate. The environment is very good, with a lake area, and the koi and black swans are particularly attractive. The set meal purchased for lunch is a seafood hot pot buffet for dinner. The cost-effectiveness is OK, and the dinner is a little expensive. Breakfast has everything it should have, and it is OK if you don't have high requirements. It's good to have a convenience store in the lobby, and you don't have to bring your own food and drinks. The water temperature of the swimming pool is 26 degrees, which is low. The badminton and table tennis courts are charged extra, and there are golf courses, rackets and balls for rent. The second floor opposite the swimming pool is a naughty castle, you have to wear socks, and it is open until 21 o'clock in the peak season, which is enough to play. It is recommended to bring children to buy a package ticket, which includes fish food, cute pet park, and non-powered park. Children love it very much. There is also a children's library in the villa area, which can be read and purchased. There are many original hardcovers. Children can stay here for half a day, but the smell of wood is a bit strong. There is a charging pile on the right side of the gate, but many fast chargers are broken. This needs to be suggested. There is nothing else. They also gave small moon cakes during the Mid-Autumn Festival. I will come again if I have the chance. I recommend everyone!
